<Review>what a great experience !! With all these money hungry businesses & rehabilitation centers, it is SO refreshing to know that there are still places out there where helping people and making a difference remains their #1 goal!!! Cedar House being one of them! <username>Patrick Flanagan<//username><Time>1616863403003<//Time><rating>1< /rating>< Review>
I have been using H&R block online tax preparation service for years and it's always been free. Great interface, friendly support staff, and easy to do your taxes year after year especially the free file option. This past year, however, I hear rumors that they are starting to charge again.

I was skeptical because I've always had such a great experience, but I called and spoke to a representative to be sure. The rep said they hadn't changed anything and for my income bracket it would be free.

After spending the 2 some odd hours to do the taxes, at the very END of this form, I find out they are trying to charge me $80 something bucks! I was pretty upset, to say the least. I don't make a lot of money, and it's been a difficult 2020 (for everyone, I'm sure). I tried  reaching out to ask why, but got nothing other than an email saying "finish your taxes today, or the price will INCREASE!!!!"

Terrified of losing out on more money I needed for rent and food, I rushed through the final process. Only to find the state taxes would cost an extra $35! FINE whatever, no organic broccoli this week we'll have the store brand stuff.

Finally finishing up with this beautiful scam website - or so I thought - when at the VERY end it turns out there's an additional $45 for "online payment transfer." That's right, something the IRS does themselves with no issue for free - H&R block CHARGES YOU FOR.

AVOID these scummy people. AVOID this scammy website. Don't give these people any more money, they're the ones lobbying Congress to keep the tax code complex!!! Save your money, I think TurboTax is still free.</Review>

Went for dinner after roughing it out in Safari West.
Was fortunate enough to land an 830pm reservation through Open Table in one shot. Score! Kobe! Apparently, they had a cancellation which worked to our benefit.
Parking was easy.
Terra is a one star Michelin fine dining establishment.  And we walked in wearing our safari outfit and converse shoes. We fit right in. Lol.
The staff in Terra are very accommodating, welcoming, and attentive. Our server always had a smile on his face whenever he addressed us.
The menu is divided into two sections -- savories and sweets. You have an option to create a four, five, or six course meal from the given selection. If you want to skip dessert, you could choose to have all savory dishes.  I didn't ask if I could have all desserts though.  Just a thought. The portions aren't minuscule either.  Gf and I opted for the 5-course tasting menu. So between us we were able to try 8 savory dishes and 2 desserts. This is a pro tip:  If you have this option, choose different items on the menu so you could try almost everything.  That is, if who you're with is willing to share.  They also had a special supplemental winter truffle menu that night.
Their food was scrumptious!  The entire meal was unbelievable!
There were obviously dishes that stood out -- chawanmushi with lobster and shrimp; saut√©ed foie gras, sweet corn soup, and truffle; lobster tortelloni, sauce am√©ricaine, shimeji mushrooms, and spinach; and, of course, their signature dish, the sake marinated black cod and shrimp dumpling, with shiso broth.
Their wine list, although California heavy (but of course we're in Napa), offers a lot of good choices at reasonable prices. Per our sommelier's recommendation, we selected the 2011 Gallica Grenache. It was a great choice.  So much so that I ended up buying 2 bottles to take home with us.
It was definitely a Terra-fic (sorry can't help it) dining experience!< /Review>

<Review>Or at least it feels like it does. It's chicken soup with grilled chicken, tortilla strips, a little bit of heat and a lot of lime, and even with a cold you can taste it, and feel it working. My friend got the Danger Dog, a bacon-wrapped hot dog in a flour tortilla with all the fixings and she was loving it. The brownie was moist and big enough to split (full disclosure -- I couldn't taste it because of my cold, but my friend said it was delish). Ordering at the counter is quick and the food comes out fast and delicious, so don't mind the line, you'll get to where you're going in time. It's one of the cheaper alternatives before a concert at the Fox or the Paramount. There's table seating on the main floor, upstairs, and a small patio outside in the back. A large-screen tv downstairs shows mostly local sports or soccer.< /Review>< Pics>

< text>
I got the NOPALES burrito and it was AMAZING! it had a spicy pumpkin seed based sauce and eggs and potatoes and delicious black refried beans and so much deliciousness. I thought it had chorizo but I was wrong and frankly, I didn't miss it at all. Would definitely order it again and recommend everyone try it at least once because it clearly has some very Mexican flavors that you don't usually get at burrito places.

Edit: I went back! It was in the afternoon so they didn't have the burrito anymore as it's only for breakfast. I'm hooked on the nopales so I got a tostada with them and also their "Lima soup" which is a super deliciously tangy limey chicken tortilla strip soup. The chicken in the soup was a little overcooked but the broth was so good I didn't mind, that broth is the broth of my dreams. The other thing could be fixed is that the chips were cold but OMG their guacamole was perfection! Highly recommend for their vegetarian/vegan options and for people who want to try some authentic Mexican cactus YUM<//text>

Xolo is my go-to place when I head to a show at the Fox. It's across the street, has delish food, is relatively inexpensive, and they are fast! My fave order consists of the Vampiro and Machaca tacos. The Vapiro taco is a cheesy corn tortilla filled with perfectly seasoned al pastor crisped to perfection. Definitely try this place out of you're into Mexican food.< /Text>
